## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / kinetic ODE modeling)
**Analysis**: The target is dA_dt, explicitly the time-derivative of a concentration A(t), which is the standard object modeled by chemical kinetics rate laws. With only (t, A) available, plausible structures are autonomous rate laws dA_dt = f(A) (reaction-order kinetics, autocatalysis, inhibition) and non-autonomous forms dA_dt = f(A, t) (time-varying rate constants, external feeding/decay, switching).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption/production: dA_dt = c0 (constant-rate source/sink over time)
- First-order decay (unimolecular): dA_dt = c0 * A (proportional to concentration; c0 typically negative for decay)
- n-th order (power-law) rate law: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general reaction order, including fractional orders)
- Second-order (bimolecular with identical reactant): dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (self-reaction / dimerization-limited kinetics)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium (first-order to A*): dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (approach to a steady concentration c1)
- Logistic/autocatalytic with carrying limit: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-amplification with depletion/limitation)
- Generalized autocatalysis: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 * (c2 - A) (flexible autocatalytic order with saturation by depletion)
- Rational inhibition (substrate inhibition-like form in A): dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate increases then saturates as A grows)
- Product inhibition / inverse dependence: dA_dt = c0 / (A + c1) (rate slows as A accumulates; useful as an empirical hindrance term)
- Mixed-order (sum of pathways): dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (parallel first- and second-order contributions)
- Time-varying first-order (k(t)A): dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * A (linearly changing effective rate constant over time)
- Periodic forcing/modulation: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * sin(c2 * t) (externally driven kinetics or oscillatory environment affecting rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Autonomous kinetics (no explicit t): if the system is well-mixed and parameters are constant, expect dA_dt to depend mainly on A via f(A).
- Reaction order identification: log-log linearity between |dA_dt| and A suggests a power-law dA_dt = c0 * A**c1; c1 near 0,1,2 correspond to classic 0th/1st/2nd order.
- Equilibrium approach: a stable steady state A = c1 typically yields a factor (c1 - A) or (A - c1) in dA_dt, implying sign change around the equilibrium.
- Autocatalysis signature: presence of an A factor multiplying a growth term (e.g., A*(c1-A)) indicates self-acceleration at low A and slowdown at high A.
- Parallel pathways: curvature in dA_dt vs A that cannot be captured by a single power suggests additive mixtures like c0*A + c1*A**2.
- Effective rate constant drift: systematic residual trends vs t at fixed A suggest k(t) (e.g., c0 + c1*t, exp(c*t), or sinusoidal modulation) multiplying an A-dependent term.
- Saturation without a hard cap: if dA_dt increases with A but plateaus, rational forms like A/(A+c1) are typical (e.g., transport/availability-limited steps).
- Inhibition by accumulation: if increasing A reduces the magnitude of dA_dt (or slows consumption), inverse-type dependence such as 1/(A+c1) can capture empirical hindrance.
- Mass-balance consistency: for pure decay/consumption, dA_dt should be non-positive across the observed A range; violations often imply source terms or time-dependent forcing.

GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.1207203443\sqrt A\;-\;0.1207203443\,A\,e^{-0.06862304899\,t}\;+\;0.8537417103\,\sin(\log(A+1)).
\]
So GT has exactly three nonconstant “shapes” in \((t,A)\):  
1) \(\sqrt A\) (no \(t\)); 2) \(A e^{kt}\) with \(k=-0.0686...\); 3) \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) (no \(t\)). No other \(A\)-dependence (no rationals, no logs outside sine, no extra constants unless zeroed).

Below, each candidate must be reducible (by choosing its free constants) to exactly that same combination for all \(t,A\).

---

### 1
Has \(A c0 e^{c1 t}\) (ok for term 2), plus \(c2 e^{A c3}\log(A c4+1)\) (cannot become \(\sqrt A\) or \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) for all \(A\) unless \(c2=0\)), plus a sine term \(c6\sin(c7\log(c8|A|+1)+c9)\) (can match \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) by setting \(c8=1,c7=1,c9=0,c6=0.8537...\) and restricting to \(A\ge0\) but equality must hold for all real \(A\); GT isn’t defined for \(A<0\) anyway due to \(\sqrt A\), so domain effectively \(A\ge0\)). Still missing \(-0.1207\sqrt A\); no way to create \(\sqrt A\) here. **No match.**

### 2
Only has \(A e^{c1 t}\) plus rational-in-\(A\) terms and \(1/(\sqrt A c5+1)\). None can equal a pure \(\sqrt A\) term for all \(A\) (the \(1/(\sqrt A c5+1)\) is not proportional to \(\sqrt A\)). No sine(log) term. **No match.**

### 3

### 4

### 5
Similar to 4: no sine, no \(\sqrt A\). **No match.**

### 6

### 7

### 11
All terms share denominator \(A^{c0}+c2\). GT has no such global denominator. Only way is to make denominator constant for all \(A\), impossible unless you force \(A^{c0}\) constant (not possible for all \(A\)) or cancel it everywhere (not possible to yield GT’s simple sum). **No match.**

You could set \(c7=0\) to remove it, but then remaining terms include \(c4 e^{A c5}\log(A c6+1)\) (must set \(c4=0\)), leaving only power terms—still no sine(log) and no \(\sqrt A\) unless via \(A^{c0}c3\) with \(c0=1/2\), but sine missing. **No match.**

### 20

Could try negative scaling and argument shift via \(c9\)? \(c9\) is inside \(\log(A c9+1)\), not an additive phase. So cannot. Also no \(\sqrt A\). **No match.**

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK15)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze each candidate against the ground truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.12072*sqrt(A) - 0.12072*A*exp(-0.06862*t) + 0.85374*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — a square root term
2. `A*exp(k*t)` — an exponential decay in t multiplied by A
3. `sin(log(A + 1))` — a sine of logarithm term

Let me check each candidate for the presence of these three basis functions.

**Key observations:**
- The `sin(log(A+c))` term is very specific. Most candidates use `log(A*c+1)` without `sin`, or rational functions, which cannot match `sin(log(...))`.
- `sqrt(A)` is also specific — it can sometimes be represented as `A^c` with `c=0.5`.
- The exponential term `A*exp(c*t)` is common in many candidates.

Let me systematically check which candidates have ALL three required basis functions:

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(A*c3)*log(A*c4+1) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*|A|+1) + c9)`
- Has `A*exp(c*t)` ✓
- Has `sin(c7*log(c8*|A|+1) + c9)` — with domain A≥0, |A|=A, so this is `sin(c7*log(c8*A+1)+c9)` ✓ (can match sin(log(A+1)) by setting c7=1, c8=1, c9=0)
- Has `exp(A*c3)*log(A*c4+1)` — need to set c2=0 to eliminate this
- Has constant c5 — set to 0
- Missing `sqrt(A)` — NO WAY to generate sqrt(A) from remaining terms

Wait, let me reconsider. If c2=0, we have `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c6*sin(log(A+1))`. Missing sqrt(A). 

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** Rational functions only, no sin(log(...)), no sqrt(A) as standalone.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** Has `sqrt(A)*c0/(sqrt(A)+c1)`, `A*c2*exp(c3*t)`, rational terms, constants. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** Has `A*c1*exp(c2*t)`, `log(A*c7+1)`, `log(A*c9+1)/A`. No sin(log(...)), no sqrt(A).
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** Similar to 4. No sin(log(...)), no sqrt(A).
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** Has `A*A^c0*c1` (can be A^(c0+1)), `A*c3*exp(c4*t)`, `A^c0*c5`, `A^c6*c7/(A^c6+c8)`. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** Has `A*c1*exp(c2*t)`, `A^c3*c4/(A^c3+c5)`, `A^c6*c7/(A^c6+c8)`. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** Has `A*c1*exp(c2*t)`, `A*c3*log(A*c4+1)`, `log(A*c7+1)`, `log(A*c9+1)/A`. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** Similar to 3. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** Has `A*c1*exp(c2*t)`, `A^c3*c4/(A^c3+c5)`, rational. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 11:** Complex rational expression. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 12:** `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*log(A*c5+1) + c6*log(A*c7+1)/A`. No sin(log(...)), no sqrt(A).
Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 13:** Same structure as 12 with extra terms. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 14:** Has `A^(2/3)`, `A^2`, `A*c3*exp(c4*t)`, `log(A*c8+1)`, `1/A^(1/3)`. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 15:** Similar to 14. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 16:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3/(A^c2+c4) + c5/(A*c6+1) + c7`. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 17:** Has `A*c7*log(c8*|A|+1)/(A+c1)`, `c9*log(c8*|A|+1)/(A+c1)`, exp(c3*t) terms. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 18:** Has `A*A^c4*c5/(A+c1)`, exp terms. No sin(log(...)).
Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 19:** `A*A^c0*c1 + A*c2 + A^c0*c3 + c4*exp(A*c5)*log(A*c6+1) + c7*log(A*c8*exp(c9*t)+1)`. No sin(log(...)). The last term `log(A*c8*exp(c9*t)+1)` mixes A and t inside log, which is fundamentally different from `A*exp(c*t)`.
Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 20:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7*cos(c8*log(A*c9+1))`
- Has `A*c2*exp(c3*t)` ✓
- Has `c7*cos(c8*log(A*c9+1))` — this is cos of log! Since sin(x) = cos(x - π/2), we need `sin(log(A+1)) = cos(log(A+1) - π/2)`. But `cos(c8*log(A*c9+1))` with c8=1, c9=1 gives `cos(log(A+1))`. We can't add a phase shift inside cos here. So this gives cos(log(A+1)), not sin(log(A+1)).

Wait — actually, `cos(c8*log(A*c9+1))`. If c9=1 and c8=1, this is `cos(log(A+1))`. But sin(log(A+1)) ≠ cos(log(A+1)) for general A. There's no phase parameter inside the cos.

However, we could try: is there a way to use the other terms? We have `c5*log(A*c6+1)` as well. But log and cos(log) are linearly independent from sin(log). So we can't construct sin(log(A+1)).

Also missing sqrt(A) — could set c0=0 and use A*c1 but that's linear in A, not sqrt(A).

Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 21:** `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A^c3*c4 + A^c5*c6 + c7 + c8*log(A*c9+1)`
- Has `A*c1*exp(c2*t)` ✓
- Has `A^c3*c4` — can be sqrt(A) with c3=0.5 ✓
- Has `A^c5*c6` — another power of A
- Has `log(A*c9+1)` — but NOT sin(log(A+1))
- No sin function at all

Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 22:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A^c4*c5 + c6 + c7*log(A*c8+1)`
- Has exp term ✓, has A^c4 (can be sqrt) ✓, but has log not sin(log).
Candidate 22 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 23:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7/(A+c8)`
- `A^c1*c2*exp(c3*t)` with c1=1 gives A*exp(c3*t) ✓
- No sin(log(...)), no sqrt(A) standalone
Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 24-50:** Let me scan for any candidate containing `sin(log(...))` or `cos(log(...))` with a phase shift possibility.

Looking through all remaining candidates... None of candidates 24-50 contain `sin` or `cos` functions except:
- Candidate 43: `c7*cos(c8*exp(A*c9))` — cos of exp, not cos of log
- Candidate 20 already checked
